[30;1m4 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m5 | [0m[35mThe entry point registry maintained by setuptools lists the available[0m
[30;1m6 | [0m[35mplugins, but does not provide a way for the end-user to control which[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35mare used or enabled. The common patterns for managing the set of[0m
[30;1m8 | [0m[35mextensions to be used are described below.[0m
[30;1m9 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m15 | [0m[35mlibrary for doing this, using ``__import__`` or ``importlib``.[0m
[30;1m16 | [0m[35mstevedore avoids creating yet another extension[0m
[30;1m17 | [0m[35mmechanism by building on top of `setuptools entry points`_. The code[0m
[30;1m18 | [0m[35mfor managing entry points tends to be repetitive, though, so stevedore[0m
[30;1m19 | [0m[35mprovides manager classes for implementing common patterns for using[0m
[30;1m20 | [0m[35mdynamically loaded extensions.[0m
